          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1167201446" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1854340497432012981"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422464265i/13504066.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>♥{<a href='https://www.blogger.com/www.eversomela.blogspot.com' rel='nofollow noopener'>Ever So Mela</a>}♥{<a href='http://www.bloglovin.com/blogs/ever-so-mela-13540125' rel='nofollow noopener'>Bloglovin</a>}♥{<a href='https://www.facebook.com/melissa.baez.94' rel='nofollow noopener'>Facebook</a>}♥{<a href='https://plus.google.com/u/0/112868988755698235218' rel='nofollow noopener'>Google+</a>}♥<br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1055489297?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Splintered Review</a><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1117938906?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Unhinged Review</a><br/><br/><b>Do you hear that sound? That gut wrenching shattering noise?</b><br/><br/>Well, <i> that would be the sound of my heart breaking</i>. The sound of my love for this series withering. The sound of death and unfulfilled dreams. The sound of darkness and gloom. Shadows and sorrow. Misery and grief.<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422733731ra/13539680.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><s>I would have so made it as an actor.</s><br/><br/><b>Ok, lets get real.</b><br/><br/><br/>This was not what I wanted. This was not how it was supposed to end. Hell NO!<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>"You can no</i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText1854340497432012981" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422464265i/13504066.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>♥{<a href="https://www.blogger.com/www.eversomela.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Ever So Mela</a>}♥{<a href="http://www.bloglovin.com/blogs/ever-so-mela-13540125" rel="nofollow noopener">Bloglovin</a>}♥{<a href="https://www.facebook.com/melissa.baez.94" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>}♥{<a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/112868988755698235218" rel="nofollow noopener">Google+</a>}♥<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1055489297?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Splintered Review</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1117938906?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Unhinged Review</a><br><br><b>Do you hear that sound? That gut wrenching shattering noise?</b><br><br>Well, <i> that would be the sound of my heart breaking</i>. The sound of my love for this series withering. The sound of death and unfulfilled dreams. The sound of darkness and gloom. Shadows and sorrow. Misery and grief.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422733731ra/13539680.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><s>I would have so made it as an actor.</s><br><br><b>Ok, lets get real.</b><br><br><br>This was not what I wanted. This was not how it was supposed to end. Hell NO!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"You can not read a book about <b>Wonderland</b> and fall for the mundane."</i>
</blockquote><br><br>A very smart friend said that and I cannot agree more. This has basically been my rant for the entire series and I will keep ranting about it every time these books are mentioned. <br><br><br><i>Funny thing is</i>, I mentally prepared myself to go into this unbiased. I didn't want to choose sides because that is-more often than not- the start of my hatred for a series. <s>The Grisha Trilogy.</s> So here I go in, thinking "I can do this. I can get over Morpheus". At least that was what I keep telling myself. But you know that little voice inside your head? The one that tells you to shut the hell up when you start spouting shit?<br><i> Well, that little sucker was on full blast. </i> <br><br>Morpheus appears and all shit spouting ended! I can't help it. He is the reason we all read this. <b>He's the character who makes the series.</b> And then he starts to make us swoon and all I could think was ways the author could kill off Jeb. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422733731i/13539681.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>But back to that in a sec.<br><br>As for the plot, I'm not the biggest fan. Even though the triangle is important for the story, for Wonderland depends on it, <b> THAT IS NO REASON FOR THIS TO BE <i>CENTERED</i> ON IT!</b> The triangle overshadows everything that resembles a plot. As for the hints of plot we do get in the story, it's excruciatingly slow. Turtle paced, slow motion <i>slow</i>. As for the scenery, it's not that bad. I mean, it's no Wonderland but at least it isn't the mortal realm again. <br><br>Then we have...<br><b>
  <u>The characters:</u>
</b><br>First let's us start off with <i>the bane of my existence</i>, aka<br><u> JEB</u> and his everlasting woe is me, spending the majority of the story being a standoff-ish ass.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403055970ra/10030052.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>He is the most whiny self-centered prick in all existence. THE WORLD DOES NO REVOLVE AROUND YOU JEB! <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422733731ra/13539682.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>He should have done us all a favor and jumped off a cliff. Or run into a sword. Or skateboarded into a bus. Or jump into shark infested water, or better piranhas. Or... You get my drift. <br>This guy is condescending, and sexist with his inability to see Alyssa as a strong female who can take care of herself. She's a Queen, you irrelevant waste of human space!<br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380371021ra/724008.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I feel he cripples the magnificence she could be if she were to choose to be full netherling. <br><br><br>Then there's <u>ALYSSA</u> and her inability to make a Goddamned choice! <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422733731ra/13539684.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>You remember that strong female lead in the first book that happened to make a disappearance in the second one? <br>Well, let me just tell you, <i>she's still in the missing person's ad. </i> <b>NOWHERE TO BE FOUND</b><br><br>Then there's all her talking a big game and what does she do? <i>Jack shit!</i>. I found her weak and indecisive. I mean, she's supposed to be <b>The Queen</b> of Wonderland and she just came across as some lovesick teenager. And yes, you don't have to tell me, I know she's in her teens but all she thought about was Jeb this and Morpheus that and gave little thought to Wonderland. It really made me question her a character. And no excuse, I wasn't <i>that dimwitted</i> as a teen. Maybe only a smudge. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380931846ra/3360272.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And finally we have glory and deprecation, sunlight and shadows. The reason we all come back. <u> MORPHEUS</u><br><br>First off<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422821137ra/13549614.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I wholeheartedly feel he's what brings uniqueness to Wonderland and therefore, this series. He's that special oomph a lot of books need and never find. He's complex and layered. And I feel he always stays true to this character. He's still manipulative and cunning but that is what draws me. Like moths to a flame&lt;&lt;&lt; See what I did there? ;)<br>Secondly, I don't think I've swoon so hard like this since Warner. And man did I swoon with Warner. But Morpheus? He is another level on his own. The things he said? Seriously he had me pausing and kissing the pages. Yes I kiss my pages, they need love ya know?<br><br>So my <b>main problem</b>-yes, besides the sheer existence of Jeb- was that ending. I felt cheated. Robbed. It was rushed, ALL THREE PAGES OF IT. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402468ra/782323.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I remember praying, because yes I even pray for good endings, that we would be graced with an epilogue. You know, a pretty little bow that ties everything neatly together. You know what they say...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422733731ra/13539685.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Dude knows what he's talking about :P<br>I can't even bring myself to say I'm surprised. This is exactly what a friend and I were talking about when we read Unhinged. But... I don't know...Sometimes it sucks to be right.<br><br><b>So in the end, it's not as horrible as I might paint it. Maybe if I hadn't gone and picked teams I would have left fascinated. But where's the fun in that?</b><br><br>I expected to be blown away but not even a gust of wind came my way :(<br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="1854340497432012981" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_849573669" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/849573669" />
    <a title="C.G. Drews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews"><img alt="C.G. Drews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1521552918p2/11375137.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/849573669?book_show_action=true">Feb 09, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="C.G. Drews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="C.G. Drews" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews">C.G. Drews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=best-of-2015">best-of-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=magical-fantasy">magical-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=retelling">retelling</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=5-star">5-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=read-2015">read-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer849573669" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6870201211555996027"><b>THE ONLY THING YOU NEED TO KNOW IS THAT THIS IS PERFECT.</b> Okay. Bye. Off you pop. Just go read it and not my review because...let's face it....I'm not going to be saying much intelligent here anyway. There will mostly be a) fangirling, b) crying, c) screeching, and d) over usage of Alice in Wonderland gifs.<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422852286ra/13554487.gif' width='400' height='224' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/>Let's get into it, shall we?<br/><br/><b>Obviously the only reason we read this book is to find out who Alyssa picks: Morpheus or Jeb?</b> I'm an aggressive Morpheus shipper. In fact, I spent the entire first </span>
  <span id="freeText6870201211555996027" style="display:none"><b>THE ONLY THING YOU NEED TO KNOW IS THAT THIS IS PERFECT.</b> Okay. Bye. Off you pop. Just go read it and not my review because...let's face it....I'm not going to be saying much intelligent here anyway. There will mostly be a) fangirling, b) crying, c) screeching, and d) over usage of Alice in Wonderland gifs.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422852286ra/13554487.gif" width="400" height="224" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>Let's get into it, shall we?<br><br><b>Obviously the only reason we read this book is to find out who Alyssa picks: Morpheus or Jeb?</b> I'm an aggressive Morpheus shipper. In fact, I spent the entire first 2 books HATING Jeb. Not being he's badly written, but because he's over-protective and squashes Alyssa and doesn't believe in her. He'd tell her not to fly in case she dies. Morpheus will literally push her off the cliff and tell her she <i>can</i> fly. Yes, Morpheus is an evil manipulative crazy narcisstic adorable moth...BUT I LOVE HIM AND I SHIP HIM AND AND...<br><br>If I'm happy you'r egoing to assume it's Morpheus/Alyssa, right? WELL. <b>Keep calm, but the love-triangle doesn't work out <i>like I thought</i> but it's still 100% perfect.</b> I'm ahppy. I AM. I'm happy because I think it was exactly what the characters woudl do. AG Howard stayed true to the characters. AND FOR THE RECORD I JUST HAPPEN TO LOVE THIS BOOK AND BE OH SO PLEASED WITH THE ENDING, DESPITE THE FACT I'M CRYING A LITTLE. Omg, It's so hard to talk about this without spoilers. Grahhhhh. SO. Don't open the spoiler section if you haven't read Ensnared or I <i>will</i> thump you. Okay? okay. <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ So it's not really a surprise how the triangle finished because they basically said how it would in Unhinged. Alyssa would pick Jeb for his mortal life and then after she grew old and he died, she would return to Wonderland and be with Morpheus for eternity. IT WAS PERFECT. I get why people would be slightly outraged...it's almost too easy. It's almost like the author couldn't decide. BUT I DON'T THINK IT'S LIKE THAT. I think the author stayed true to the characters (gah, I keep repeating that, but it's just what I think, yes?) and everyone made huge sacrifices. Morpheus agreed to wait 80 or so years. He didn't ahve to. BUT HE DID BECAUSE HE LOVES ALYSSA. And Jeb agreed to know that when he'd die, Alyssa would live forever with Morpheus. He agreed to it. And Alyssa, who looks like she has a 1000% win-win situation here, signed up for eternity with 2 drama queens, so I think she's being punished sufficiently. I'm happy that Alyssa got both the guys. Gah. It sounds like a harem, but but but...MORPHEUS FOREVER. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422852286ra/13554488.gif" width="423" height="270" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The writing is beautiful as ever.</b> Wonderland is such a beautiful, feral and awesomely described place. I was sucked into this book. LITERALLY SUCKED IN. I was so engrossed. I had to read a little slower (usually my speed is like super-super fast) so I could catch all the detail, but I loved it. I loved the attention. I loved the vivid writing. A lot of the book is set in AnyElsewhere...I wasn't sure if that was Wonderland or not (it's been a year since Unhinged), but I think it's NOT. It's like some sort of hellish version of Wanderland. ANYWAY. It was gorgeous and freaky and nasty and entrancing. <br><br><b>The threesome were epic as always.</b> GUESS WHAT!? I DON'T HATE JEB ANYMORE! I actually have a ton of respect for him after this book, and I really admire his sacrifices and what he went through and the pain and his artistic side. Like seriously, how many books are there about guys who would punch as soon as look at you, AND are wickedly talentedly artistic?? It's awesome. Jeb's attitude bugs me...but...he and Morpheus have quite the relationship in this book. IT'S ADORABLE. They actually come to an understanding. As for Alyssa, she let's out her wild cruel streak and does quite a few questionable things. She's still a bit of a fainting damsel, but I don't even care. She did EVERYTHING to save Wonderland <i>and</i> those she loved. Alyssa is a hero. She's amazing. She's the kind of heroine I want to read about.<br><br>(The parents are in the book but they mostly got ditched. I'm not complaining...but that <i>is</i> a bit of a YA stereotype that you can't have a real adventure with your parents. But NOT COMPLAINING because I wanted Jeb/Morpheus/Alyssa NOT the parents anyway. Though her dad is rather awesome.)<br><br><b>Basically I shall scream and flail and be OH SO HAPPY with this finale.</b> It couldn't be more perfect, really. The ending is satisfiying but leaves me crying because <i>I want mooooore</i>. I will miss Wonderland like nothing else. I WILL MISS THE MOTH. OH MY MORPHEUS. He was so perfect from beginning to end. Snarky and quirky. I love his clothes too. And...and....oh <b>this book surprised me no end, it even ripped out my heart at one point and left me squinting at the page going "noooooo wut. nooooo". BUT IT WAS PERFECT AND I AM HAPPY.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422852387ra/13554491.gif" width="500" height="233" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>QUOTES OF NOTABLE AWESOME:</b><br><br>I look back at Dad, who's keeping us in his sight from a few steps behind. "Put yourself in his place. Can you imagine what he's been through? The nightmares he's had to relive and accept as reality over the past few hours?"<br>Several steps ahead of me now, Morpheus lifts his head, letting the humid breeze ripple the blue fringe at the edges of his hat. "Yes, poor fellow. Must've been unbearable, realising how much the woman he adores loves him back."<br>Flapping my wings, I match his swift pace. "You can't possibly compare their romance to..."<br>He appraises my face, wearing a wry smile. "To whose, Alyssa?"<br><br>*<br><br>Dad crosses to where we are, obviously distracted by our joined hands. "What are we stopping for?"<br>Morpheus scowls. "Simply waiting for the human to catch up, whilst knowing that he never truly will," he quips, cool as always.<br><br>* <br><br>Jeb huffs. "Uh-huh. Sit up here so I can fix your ear. I have a painting to finish."<br>The domestic undertone of their interactions is so fascinating it makes me pause. I wonder how long they've been holed up here together. For the entire time they've been trapped in this realm? <br><br>* <br><br>I shake my head. "I don't care what's on your hands. Please look at me. I missed you. I was so worried about you."<br>"Really? Which one of us are you talking to?" His attention crosses to Morpheus, who smirks conspiratorially. <br>Even more unsettling than seeing the guys on the same side of anything is having them gang up on me. <br><br>*<br><br>"Go back to your room, Morpheus." Jeb takes the paintbrush. "The grown-ups have work to do."<br>Morpheus tilts his head to meet my gaze from behind the frame. "Aw, shy little blossom. You should've seen the atrocities he tried to put me in those first few days. He didn't let me have a say until I walked around naked for a few hours. Should you decide to employ that strategy, I'll be behind you one hundred percent. Or in front of you. Lady's choice." He winks.<br><br>*<br><br>"Birds of a feather. Yada yada yada. The cliche is kind of boring."<br>"I rather like to think of us more as moths of a flame. And trying to predict which one of us might get burned first is far from boring, luv." (pg. 199)<br><br>*<br><br>By and by, using a toy diary enchanted by a child's love-magic to hold repudiated memories at a safe distance...bloody brilliant. If I weren't already head over heels for you, that stunt would've pulled the rug out from under me and left me flailing flat on my back." (pg. 203)<br><br>*<br><br>"My precious Alyssa, share reality with me. Give me forever. We will wreck such beautiful havoc together."<br><br>*<br><br>"Right," Jeb scoffs. "Pretty sure my mistreatment wouldn't have sent you into hysterics, drama queen."<br>Morpheus smirks. "Fair enough. On the other hand, your portrayal of a brainless wind-up numbskull was spot on."<br>Jeb's lips quiver, as if he's fighting a smile himself. "You know, I still have enough paint to make that flyswatter."</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="6870201211555996027" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15749291-hannah-the-curiouser-curiouser?shelf=i-want-to-eat-the-writing">i-want-to-eat-the-writing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15749291-hannah-the-curiouser-curiouser?shelf=hot-hot">hot-hot</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer860000482" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1414518095947009424"><b>Updated: 3/21/2015</b><br/><br/>Rating: 5 (bloody brilliant) stars.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426984962ra/14153432.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Bloody <i>brilliant</i>, I’ll say.<br/><br/>Now, I realize this book has become a hot topic in a hate/love war. I get it. I do. And after reading the book, I understand the angst, anger, and everything in-between.<br/><br/>But let me say this, because I realize that I won’t be able to write this review without possibly seriously offending some people and/or making them question my morals in life: <b>I just don’t really care.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426984962ra/14153433.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Feel free to disagree with me. (I’m being complet</span>
  <span id="freeText1414518095947009424" style="display:none"><b>Updated: 3/21/2015</b><br><br>Rating: 5 (bloody brilliant) stars.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426984962ra/14153432.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Bloody <i>brilliant</i>, I’ll say.<br><br>Now, I realize this book has become a hot topic in a hate/love war. I get it. I do. And after reading the book, I understand the angst, anger, and everything in-between.<br><br>But let me say this, because I realize that I won’t be able to write this review without possibly seriously offending some people and/or making them question my morals in life: <b>I just don’t really care.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426984962ra/14153433.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Feel free to disagree with me. (I’m being completely serious.) That’s totally fine, but I’m just giving ya’ll the heads up: this is a very, very positive review.<br><br><b>I’m going to write this spoiler free, BTW.</b> Just so you know and aren’t scared of being COMPLETELY RUINED TO THE ENDING OF THIS TRILOGY.<br><br>(*clears throat*)<br><br>Sorry. As you can probably guess, this is what happened to me before I even got my hands on the book.<br><br>Which might have had something to do with how I’m handling the ending now, since I’ve just finished it. Had I not been spoiled, maybe I’d be reacting differently.<br><br>When I first learned of the ending (again, I strongly encourage you NOT to be spoiled, however tempting it may be) I didn’t really know what to think. I knew right then the ending was going to be one of the best things to ever happen or one of the worst and will completely ruin the series for me.<br><br>But, alas, I find I’m very happy with how it all ended.<br><br><br><pre>
  <i>As if waiting for that signal, he releases my hands, cups my face, and whispers in my ear. “My precious Alyssa, share reality with me. Give me forever. We will wreak such beautiful havoc together.”</i>
</pre><br><br>Am I still a little confused? Sure, a little. But also, I get why Alyssa made the decision that she did. I really do and my opinion of her has changed because of it. I don’t see her as being selfish, but I do understand why so many readers now see her that way.<br><br>The ending is very, very unique, and, honestly, one heck of a gutsy move. I can only think of one other book that had a very similar ending, and just as I did not have a problem with it then, I do not have a problem with it here.<br><br>What I think is this: <b>the decisions Alyssa makes in this final novel weren’t made alone.</b> Jeb and Morpheus were right there next to her and gave her their blessing. Not because they were tricked into it, not because they didn’t understand everything they were agreeing to. They saw their options, and all three of them of them understood and were okay with their choice.<br><br>I’m a huge <i>Alice in Wonderland</i> fan (read: <i>obviously</i>). If you didn’t know that about me, you really should. (Again, how is this not obvious?)<br><br>So I don’t say I’m happy with how this series ended lightly. Alice is one of my favorite childhood characters and if an author ever tries to do a retelling of it and fails, I have <b><i>no</i> mercy</b>. None. I will rip that book apart with my teeth.<br><br><pre>
  <i>“Jebediah has given up on you, but I never will. I can offer you the security you desire. If you’ll but be mine, your heart will forever be sheltered in my care. Yes, we will quarrel incessantly and fight for dominance. And yes, there will be ravishes of passion, but there will also be gentle lulls. That is who we are together. You’ll never need fear that your love is not reciprocated. For although you’ve made me feel things I am not equipped for . . . I cannot stop feeling them."</i>
</pre><br><br><b>I love Morpheus.</b> I’ve said it before and I’ll say it again. He’s one of my favorite male leads.<br><br>He’s just so <i>wicked</i>.<br><br>I was really prepared for the worst going into this book. Partly because I was spoiled and partly because I wasn’t as impressed with <i>Unhinged</i> as I was with <i>Splintered</i>. I saw this series as starting off amazingly great but then going downhill.<br><br>I am so pleasantly surprised.<br><br><pre>
  <i>“You opened Pandora’s box within me. Set loose the imaginings and emotions of a mortal man. And there is no closing it ever again.” The jewels under his eyes twitch between dark purple and blue. “As much as I abhor being anything akin to human, Alyssa, I wouldn’t dare try to close it. Because that would mean losing you.”</i>
</pre><br><br>I love that Alyssa is able to love both Morpheus and Jeb equally (as much as I abhor Jeb). There is no choosing between them. <b>I love that Alyssa understands that there is no changing Morpheus, that to love him is to love even the downright cunning, most wicked parts of him.</b> She does not make him gentle, docile. She makes him even more crazy and cunning. Just as he does to her.<br><br>I even love that Alyssa loves Jeb without ever wishing he were a little more like Morpheus – magical and unruly. She loved them both for the things that make them differently, but she’s able to love them equally, which is no small thing.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426984962ra/14153434.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And that’s so glorious.<br><br>So <i>bravo,</i>, Ms. Howard. Bravo, indeed.<br><br>Find me here: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://obsessivereads.wordpress.com/">https://obsessivereads.wordpress.com/</a><br><br>_______________________________________________________________________<br><br>My feels . . . THE FEELS AFTER THE ENDING OF <i>UNHINGED</i>!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1401774313ra/9845962.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jeb? Jeb who? You say he’s on the cover, and all the fangirls are going crazy?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1401774313ra/9845963.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Give me Morpheus, gosh darn it! The world of <i>Splintered</i> only makes sense if he’s there!! I only care about him being with Alyssa!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1401774313ra/9845964.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Check out my blog here, where I also fangirl over YA books: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://obsessivereads.wordpress.com/">http://obsessivereads.wordpress.com/</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="1414518095947009424" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6970283582773743786"><br/>I’m blessed to have read an early draft of ENSNARED. There’s no better gift, so thank you to the moon and back, Tooth Fairy!<br/><br/>Anita wrote an escapist's dream series. The SPLINTERED series is fantasy—wildly beautiful fantasy—but don’t assume that the books lack depth because they’re madly twisted. The characters make tragic, crazy, and sometimes even wise choices. The flaws make the characters, in my opinion, just as much as the triumphs.<br/>But Anita's ability to stay true to her story is what leaves </span>
  <span id="freeText6970283582773743786" style="display:none"><br />I’m blessed to have read an early draft of ENSNARED. There’s no better gift, so thank you to the moon and back, Tooth Fairy!<br /><br />Anita wrote an escapist's dream series. The SPLINTERED series is fantasy—wildly beautiful fantasy—but don’t assume that the books lack depth because they’re madly twisted. The characters make tragic, crazy, and sometimes even wise choices. The flaws make the characters, in my opinion, just as much as the triumphs.<br />But Anita's ability to stay true to her story is what leaves her mark upon readers.<br />I won't spoil the story or let slip the deets on whether #JebJunkies or #MothMinions will rejoice, but I will tell you this: Alyssa's choices in ENSNARED showcase how much her character has grown throughout the series…<br />This final novel doesn’t have a perfectly-tied bow atop a classic fairy-tale ending; fitting inside a pristinely wrapped box just wouldn’t suit Al, as we all know. Instead, she took her fate in her own hands, and I think most fans will delight in where she ended the story.<br />I know I did.<br /><br />Oh, and Mothy is as hawt as ever</span>

<div id="review_789736564" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/789736564" />
    <a title="Jessi (Novel Heartbeat)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6759885-jessi-novel-heartbeat"><img alt="Jessi (Novel Heartbeat)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1491529769p2/6759885.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/789736564?book_show_action=true">Dec 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessi (Novel Heartbeat)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessi (Novel Heartbeat)" href="/user/show/6759885-jessi-novel-heartbeat">Jessi (Novel Heartbeat)</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6759885-jessi-novel-heartbeat?shelf=cover-lust">cover-lust</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6759885-jessi-novel-heartbeat?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer789736564" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7615882531849698352"><a href='http://novelheartbeat.com' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419949228i/13149855.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>What a glorious end to an amazing series!! I really enjoyed it, but I’m very sad to see it go. I can’t believe I’ll never see Morph again :(<br/><br/>I was so thrilled to jump back into the world that Howard creates! I didn’t realize how much I’d missed it. It’s sooo twisted…I love it! There were certain scenes where I was just like …..<i>creeeeeepyyy</i>…… and ok, I was a little disturbed. <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[Um, the talking punching bag of Jeb’s dad? Creepy! All of Jeb’s paintings were sooo cool, though! I love</span></span>
  <span id="freeText7615882531849698352" style="display:none"><a href="http://novelheartbeat.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419949228i/13149855.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>What a glorious end to an amazing series!! I really enjoyed it, but I’m very sad to see it go. I can’t believe I’ll never see Morph again :(<br><br>I was so thrilled to jump back into the world that Howard creates! I didn’t realize how much I’d missed it. It’s sooo twisted…I love it! There were certain scenes where I was just like …..<i>creeeeeepyyy</i>…… and ok, I was a little disturbed. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Um, the talking punching bag of Jeb’s dad? Creepy! All of Jeb’s paintings were sooo cool, though! I love the idea of Red’s and Morpheus’s magic blending together to make Jeb’s.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>MORPHEUS. OMG. How I love him!! As always, I was blown away by his depth of caring for Alyssa. There was absolutely nothing that he wouldn’t do for her! And most of all, he recognized her strength. As I mentioned in my review of <i>Unhinged</i>, he never doubted that she could handle herself. He didn’t save her all the time because he knew she could save herself. I loved that!!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“I finally have a secret of my own. Not so fun being on the other side of one, is it?”<br>The slow burn of amusement warms his features. He leans in and whispers, “On the contrary, My Queen. I cannot imagine anything more delicious than peeling away your defenses, layer by layer, baring your precious….secret.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384398598ra/6867318.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Um, and let’s not even talk about him making Alyssa lingerie out of his prom outfit. *dies* I should <i>probably</i> find that disturbing, but it’s actually kinda sexy O_O <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>And then we have Jeb. Oh, little Jeb. It’s no secret that I am NOT a Jeb fan. And in the beginning, I kind of hated him. He was really digging that hole! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[It pissed me off that he believed for certain that Alyssa wouldn’t come for him, whereas Morpheus had faith in her. He was proud of her for finding a way. Then, the animosity that Jeb showed Alyssa, despite all that she’d gone through to get back to him, made me dislike him even more.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> However, toward the end I do have to admit that he earned my grudging respect. *heavy sigh* I <i>suppose</i> he was alright in the end. (But Morpheus is still better!)<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I loved how everything was handled with the final showdown! I was pretty darn shocked when they revealed that “Jeb” had his eyes and tongue cut out. I was like Wait, what?! No way. They’ll fix it somehow. Then he got thrown into the acid fountain, and I knew there had to be something else going on. No way would Jeb die! (And wait, do I actually care about that?! What is happening?!) I totally didn’t even think about his double! I also thought it was awesome that Jeb repainted Wonderland! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <br>The ending made me cry a little! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[HAPPY tears!! It was so beautiful, you guys! It’s so rare for a book to make me cry because it’s happy, not sad (um, someone dying). That gets bonus points from me! I thought it was perfect! Although, I can see where people could have a problem with it. Despite the fact that I loved it, I still have my reservations about it morally. It doesn’t quite sit well with me that Alyssa got the best of both worlds. It doesn’t work that way!! But this is fantasy and I do enjoy a HEA as much as the next girl does!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>Favorite quote:</b><br><br><i>Glory and deprecation – sunlight and shadows – the scuttle of a scorpion and the melody of a nightingale. Sister One’s description of him never seemed more apt. The breath of the sea and the cannonade of a storm. </i><br><br><b>This review was originally posted on <a href="http://novelheartbeat.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Novel Heartbeat</a>. To see a breakdown of my assessment, please visit the full review on my blog.</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15203610615913911019">What an amazing ending for an amazing series.<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1399815086ra/9599045.gif' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Now that Alyssa managed to shun all the neatherlings from the human world, she has to return to Wonderland for the final battle between her and Queen Red and more importantly for rescuing the people that she loved.<br/>Before she does that however she has to find a way to get back since the rabbit hole vanished.<br/>So she has to get help from the only person that knows his way around Wonderland better than anyone. Someone that managed to go through the human W</i></span>
  <span id="freeText15203610615913911019" style="display:none">What an amazing ending for an amazing series.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1399815086ra/9599045.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Now that Alyssa managed to shun all the neatherlings from the human world, she has to return to Wonderland for the final battle between her and Queen Red and more importantly for rescuing the people that she loved.<br>Before she does that however she has to find a way to get back since the rabbit hole vanished.<br>So she has to get help from the only person that knows his way around Wonderland better than anyone. Someone that managed to go through the human World to elsewhere to Wonderland without any help.<br><br>With the help of her father, Alyssa finds herself once again infront of Queen Red and this time she will make sure that she will win the battle once and for all.</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1489613028i/22232295._SX540_.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>The first thing that draw me to this series, was the book covers.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1489613028i/22232296._SX540_.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>I mean... look at them.... they're gorgeous!<br><br>Still, I was apprehensive about picking them up since it wasn't really a popular series and the people who had read them, weren't really thrilled with it.<br>So I had this awkward dance with them contemplating about buying them and then I did.<br><br>They still were sitting on my shelf for a couple of years before I finally started reading them and <b>Oh.My.God. Why hadn't I started them sooner?</b><br><br><br>• <u>The Story</u> combined the original books by Lewis Caroll with it's own unique plot that had just taken the perfect amount of the first ones and shaped them into a entire different story.<br><br>It had quite a bit of madness into it and had it's dark moments, but not enough to give you the creeps.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1478623325ra/21092280.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br>• <u>The characters</u> were well written. <i>(Another "villain" that you just have to love more than the "nice guy". <br>*cough* Aleksander Morozova*cough*)</i><br><br>It isn't another remake of Alice Liddell going through the rabbit hole, but her great-great-granddaughter (or something).<br><br><br>•<u>Wonderland</u> and it's creatures weren't the fluffy, happy, mad, cute little animals who could talk.<br>Well... they were mad (who isn't ;)) <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489613028ra/22232294.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>but they were everything but fluffy, happy or cute.<br>They were more like gory, creepy little humanoid things.<br><br><br>I basically loved everything about this series and if you're looking for an amazing Alice in Wonderland retelling, look no further.<br><br><b>And if you have read or seen or heard of.... another Alice retelling... Please let me know! :D Thank you.</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489613028ra/22232293.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1042771778" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9976088459469151560">I was lucky enough to be spoiled by Anita and I got to read the MS right after she was finished writing it. After final edits were done, I got to read it again. Let me tell you, this book was absolute perfection. <br/><br/>There are swoons and laughs and action and heartfail and so many creepy things that it's like a delicious roller coaster. There were scenes that I wanted to squeeze my laptop in joy and then pages later throw it across the room while screaming. <br/><br/>Alyssa, Jeb, Morpheus, and all of the othe</span>
  <span id="freeText9976088459469151560" style="display:none">I was lucky enough to be spoiled by Anita and I got to read the MS right after she was finished writing it. After final edits were done, I got to read it again. Let me tell you, this book was absolute perfection. <br /><br />There are swoons and laughs and action and heartfail and so many creepy things that it's like a delicious roller coaster. There were scenes that I wanted to squeeze my laptop in joy and then pages later throw it across the room while screaming. <br /><br />Alyssa, Jeb, Morpheus, and all of the other characters are just so fantastic. I want to climb into the rabbit hole and go to tea parties with them. Alyssa's journey and growth through the series has been fantastic, it's been such a delight being in her head. <br /><br />As for the ending? There aren't even words. I'm a million percent positive that it couldn't have been done any differently or any better. <br /><br />Thank you, Anita. Not only for spoiling me {which I love}, but for taking us on this amazingly mad ride.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/969704230?book_show_action=true">Jun 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Clarissa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Clarissa" href="/user/show/21942964-clarissa">Clarissa</a>

          marked it as to-read




        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer969704230" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7038109483999823451">LOVE the colours on this, but ugh Jeb. Why, can't we just have another Morpheus cover... I'd be down for that *swoon*. <br/>I'm currently in the middle of Ruin and Rising by Leigh Bardugo and I got to talking with a friend of mine and I feel slightly more worried going into this book now. <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ Even though they're two completely different characters (and I think it's safe to say the Darkling is more "obviously" evil than Morpheus is), the way that Alyssa views Morpheus is SO similar to how </span></span>
  <span id="freeText7038109483999823451" style="display:none">LOVE the colours on this, but ugh Jeb. Why, can't we just have another Morpheus cover... I'd be down for that *swoon*. <br />I'm currently in the middle of Ruin and Rising by Leigh Bardugo and I got to talking with a friend of mine and I feel slightly more worried going into this book now. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Even though they're two completely different characters (and I think it's safe to say the Darkling is more "obviously" evil than Morpheus is), the way that Alyssa views Morpheus is SO similar to how Alina saw the Darkling that it's impossible not to draw parallels. <br /><br />After hearing the way that Ruin and Rising turns out *gags* I feel more worried than ever at the prospect of a Malina esque ending with Jeb and Alyssa being endgame. Again this relationship is just one of those situations where it's so much more than a simple disliking for one of the points of the love triangle (even though like with Mal, I detest Jeb aussi). You simply have to look at the way Alyssa is with the both of these guys and there's just no comparing who she could be and the life she could live if she ends up with Morpheus, or even just ends up on her own for crying out loud. To me Jeb parallels Mal to a tee, and that bothers me, it bothers me a lot. <br /><br />Let's just say that after the way that R &amp; R is turning out I'm starting to see parallels in this book as well. I dislike the childhood friends turned lovers trope and it just does nothing for me. I like mystery, darkness, and complexity in my characters. I like to question what truly encapsulates good and what defines evil and I don't like characters taking the easy way out (which is exactly what I feel happened to Alina with Mal in R &amp; R).<br /> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br /><br />Rant done, but at this point it looks like I'll just have to be a bit more hesitant by the time this book rolls around. I trust you A.G Howard... I trust you got my feels (hopefully) right? </span>

<div id="review_1642185756" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1642185756" />
    <a title="Irene△⃒⃘➰" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/55991704-irene"><img alt="Irene△⃒⃘➰" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603216583p2/55991704.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1642185756?book_show_action=true">Sep 22, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Irene△⃒⃘➰" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Irene△⃒⃘➰" href="/user/show/55991704-irene">Irene△⃒⃘➰</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9788854190870" href="/book/show/29539878-il-segreto-della-regina-rossa">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/55991704-irene?shelf=read-in-2017">read-in-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/55991704-irene?shelf=cover-love">cover-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1642185756" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15994642578840386053"><b>4.6/5</b> ~ ITA/ENG (NOW ADDED)<br/><br/><i>
  <blockquote>"Sono il vento<br/>Sono la furia<br/>Sono il pandemonio"</blockquote>
</i><br/><br/>Si conclude (anche se c'è ancora un libro e una novella) questa avventura pazzesca di Alyssa.<br/><b>Il mondo di questo Paese delle Meraviglie pazzo mi è piaciuto tantissimo.</b> <br/>E' sicuramente il punto di forza di questi libri.<br/>Mi è piaciuta poi l'impostazione dove senza dirlo in modo esplicito si capisce che <b>ogni libro si concentra maggiormente su uno dei nostri tre personaggi principali.</b><br/>Nel primo abbiamo tutta l'avventura di Alys</span>
  <span id="freeText15994642578840386053" style="display:none"><b>4.6/5</b> ~ ITA/ENG (NOW ADDED)<br /><br /><i>
  <blockquote>"Sono il vento<br />Sono la furia<br />Sono il pandemonio"</blockquote>
</i><br /><br />Si conclude (anche se c'è ancora un libro e una novella) questa avventura pazzesca di Alyssa.<br /><b>Il mondo di questo Paese delle Meraviglie pazzo mi è piaciuto tantissimo.</b> <br />E' sicuramente il punto di forza di questi libri.<br />Mi è piaciuta poi l'impostazione dove senza dirlo in modo esplicito si capisce che <b>ogni libro si concentra maggiormente su uno dei nostri tre personaggi principali.</b><br />Nel primo abbiamo tutta l'avventura di Alyssa, accompagnata da Morpheus e Jeb, sel secondo c'è Morpheus e nel terzo c'è Jeb.<br /><b>Tra i tre quello di Jeb è stato il mio preferito. Ho amato il mondo che la Howard ha costruito per lui, il concetto dei graffiti e delle varie porte.</b><br />Tutto quanto è così vivido nella mia mente perchè <b>le descrizioni sono veramente dettagliate</b>, non noiose, e piene di particolari che incuriosiscono sempre più.<br /><br />Questo ultimo libro nello specifico è <b>un po' lentino</b>, ovviamente tranne verso la fine. Si parte col botto dove ci si era lasciati nello scorso, ma conclusa quella piccola pre-avventura si è un po' calmato.<br />Non è mai stato troppo noioso, solo che <b>mi aspettavo che venisse data più rilevanza alla storia di Rossa e "dell'ultima battaglia".</b><br />Nel centro <b>si è dilungato abbastanza sulla solita storia Alyssa vs Morpheus vs Jeb</b> che sì ci può stare, ma dopo un po' ha inizianto a stancarmi un pochettino.<br /><br />Lo stile di scrittura era okay, <b>non sono una fan in generale dello stile della Howard</b> mi sa, ma non ho avuto troppi problemi nel collegarmi, probabilmete perchè la storia attira parecchio e la scrittura passa in secondo piano, almeno per me.<br /><br />Che dire poi del finale, <b>L'EPILOGO mi ha uccisa</b>. E' stato bellissimo vedere come alla fine tutto si incastra perfettamente e non restano domande non risposte. <br /><b>Ho trovato proprio le ultime pagine emozionanti ed eccitanti</b>, la storia non resta sospesa ma si conclude, e lo ritengo un <b>finale perfetto</b> per questa serie piena di creature e personaggi fantastici (in tutti i sensi!).<br />_________________________<br /><br />And I reached the end (even if there's still a book and a novella to read) of this mad adventure of Alyssa.<br /><b>I loved the world of this crazy Wonderland</b>. It's absolutely the strenght of these books.<br />I liked that even if it's not said directly, you can guess (by the covers too) that <b>every book focuses on one of our main characters.</b><br />In the first one, there's all the very first adventure of Alyssa (accompanied by Morpheus and Jeb), in the second one there's Morpheus and in this last one Jeb.<br /><b>Out of the three Jeb's is the one I liked the most. I loved the world that Howard created for him, the whole graffiti and various doors concept.</b><br />Everything is so vivid in my head thanks to those <b>very rich descriptions</b>, not boring and full of little details that intrigue you more and more.<br /><br />This last book specificly <b>is a little slow</b>, not towards the finale obviously. It started straight away where we previously left, but once that very beginning full of action ended, it quieted down a little bit.<br />It was never too boring but <b>I hoped it would have been given to all the Queen Red's backstory and final battle a lot more space and relevance.</b><br />In the middle <b>it dwelled a lot with all the Alyssa vs Morpheus vs Jeb drama</b>, that after a while started to unnerve me a little.<br /><br />The writing style was okay, I think that <b>I'm not a fan of Howard's writing style</b> but I never had problems in connecting the events, probably because the story is too exciting and the writing style wasn't that relevant, at least for me.<br /><br />What to say about that finale, <b>THE EPILOGUE killed me</b>. It was so cool seeing how everything matches perfectly and there are no questions unanswered.<br /><b>I found the very last pages very emotional and exciting</b>, the story is not left suspended but <b>it ends with a finale that I think was perfect</b> for this series full of fantastic creatures and people!</span>
  <a data-text-id="15994642578840386053" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('IeQdUFcBbJ0qPfPU0P3CLHumrktsItJfehxHkVU5hadwwctApi6RUH3T38Myd/WKGEj/3N6SFAXz5gd7+e3FUg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('PKjK8TmIJQEEY0ez5CZCv5ZHJbC1G557dSjCbFIvJSdtjRzhyKfYzFONa6QGrHUZ9al0JwerWCH80oKG/vtl0g==')})
  }
//]]>

<span id="freeTextContainer14976889811527532908">#1 New York Times and International bestselling Author of gothic / fantasy & paranormal tales, mystical & romantic with a side of horror. A.G.'s dark Alice in Wonderland inspired Splintered series has been published in over a dozen languages. <br/><br/>Young adult, Adult, and literary romance. Repped by Jenny Bent.<br/><br/>How A.G. Howard rates books on GoodReads:<br/><br/>"I only rate or review books I enjoyed reading, and w</span>
  <span id="freeText14976889811527532908" style="display:none">#1 New York Times and International bestselling Author of gothic / fantasy &amp; paranormal tales, mystical &amp; romantic with a side of horror. A.G.'s dark Alice in Wonderland inspired Splintered series has been published in over a dozen languages. <br /><br />Young adult, Adult, and literary romance. Repped by Jenny Bent.<br /><br />How A.G. Howard rates books on GoodReads:<br /><br />"I only rate or review books I enjoyed reading, and won't give any rating below 4 stars. Please don't consider every high rating a personal endorsement / recommendation from me. My ratings here are subjective to me as an individual. <br /><br />I don't rate books solely on style. Every writer's voice is individual and unique; I've come to respect this truth during my own personal journey. As long as a story takes me to another place and is well edited, I'm going to give it a good rating. And if, for some reason, a book doesn't entertain me or I don't finish it, I won't leave a rating or review at all. <br /><br />If you're considering a book I've reviewed/rated, be sure to read other reviews/ratings alongside mine to help you decide if it's a read you might enjoy personally.<br /><br />Happy book hunting!"<br /><br /></span>
